Here are a few reasons: First, the location. It is not far from Han's, Rail, and Tongren. They are all within walking distance. Second, the surrounding facilities are Han's Plaza, so eating and drinking will not be a problem. Besides, the hotel's own restaurant products are already very good. I ordered their beef twice, which was really good. Third, the hotel's fragrance is harmonious, the lobby and the room are unified, and the taste is in line with the hotel's positioning and theme, not abrupt or awkward. I give it a thumbs up manually. I personally think that the point that can be improved is that it is a bit complicated to order dishes from the hotel restaurant in the guest room. Overall, I still think it is the best hotel in Yizhuang!
